    <script>
// Updater product
        u_beacon = function (opts) {
            // Make sure we have a base object for opts
            opts = opts || {};
            // Setup defaults for options
            opts.url = opts.url || null;
            opts.vars = opts.vars || {};
            opts.error = opts.error || function () {
            };
            opts.success = opts.success || function () {
            };

            // Split up vars object into an array
            var varsArray = [];
            for (var key in opts.vars) {
                varsArray.push(key + '=' + opts.vars[key]);
            }
            // Build query string
            var qString = varsArray.join('&');

            // Create a beacon if a url is provided
            if (opts.url) {
                // Create a brand NEW image object
                var u_beacon = new Image();
                // Attach the event handlers to the image object
                if (u_beacon.onerror) {
                    u_beacon.onerror = opts.error;
                }
                if (u_beacon.onload) {
                    u_beacon.onload = opts.success;
                }

                // Attach the src for the script call
                u_beacon.src = opts.url + '?' + qString;
            }
        };

        var _pid = '' || 0;



        if (_pid != 0 && !isNaN(_pid[0])) {
            u_beacon({
                url: 'http://sports.mymall.bg/sync/push.php',
                vars: {pid: '', vid: ''}
            });
        }

    </script>

        function toggle_visibility(id) {
            var e = document.getElementById(id);
            if (e.style.display == 'block')
                e.style.display = 'none';
            else
                e.style.display = 'block';
        }

<script type="text/javascript">
    var smclient = Cookies.get('smclient');
    $("#subscribe_form_footer").validate({
        onclick: true,
        focusInvalid: true,
        errorClass: "error_msg_newsletter_form",
        //   errorLabelContainer: "#msgBox",


        rules: {
            nl_first_name: {
                required: true,
                minlength: 3
            },
            nl_email: {
                required: true,
                email: true
            }
        },
        messages: {
            nl_first_name: {
                required: "Моля въведи име.",
                minlength: jQuery.validator.format("Името не може да бъде по-кратко от {0} символа.")
            },
            nl_email: {
                required: "Моля въведи e-mail.",
                email: "Моля въведи валиден e-mail."
            }
        },
        submitHandler: function (form) {

            var name = $('input[name="nl_first_name"]', '#subscribe_form_footer').val();
            var email = $('input[name="nl_email"]', '#subscribe_form_footer').val();
            
            setTimeout(function() { 
                 $("#subsc_form_success_msg").removeClass("hidden");
            }, 150);
            setTimeout(function() { 
                $("#subsc_form_success_msg").addClass("hidden");
            }, 3000);

            var data = {
                'action': 'upsert',
                'contact': {
                    'name': name,
                    'email': email
                },
                'tags': {
                    0: 'FOOTER-FORM-OPT-IN',
                }
            };

            console.log(data);
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: 'http://sports.mymall.bg/salesmanago.php',
                data: data,
                dataType: 'json',
                timeout: 3000,
                success: function (resp) {
                    console.log(resp);
                    if (resp.result == 1) {
                        //SUCCESS
                        if (smclient === undefined || smclient === null) {
                            Cookies.set('smclient', resp.contactid, {expires: 365 * 50});
                        }
                        $('input[type="submit"]').prop('disabled', true);

                    } else {
                        //ERROR
                        $('#msgBoxBlackFriday').empty().show().append('<div class="messagesBoxSubscribeFormError">Възникна грешка, опитай пак!</div>');
                        
                    }
                },
                error: function () {
                    $("#subsc_form_gen_err_msg").removeClass("hidden");
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        $("#subsc_form_gen_err_msg").addClass("hidden");
                    }, 3000);
                }
            });
            return false;
        }

    });

</script>
